	function includeStyleScript(url, tag, onload){
		tag = tag.toLowerCase();
		var found = false;
		var linkScript = document.getElementsByTagName(tag);
		for(var i = 0; i < linkScript.length; i++){
			var urlTest = (linkScript[i].href) ? linkScript[i].href : linkScript[i].src;
			if(urlTest==url){ found=true; break; }
		}
		if(found == false){
			if(tag == "link"){
				var lnk = document.createElement('link'), head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || document.documentElement;
				lnk.rel     = 'stylesheet';
				lnk.type    = 'text/css';
				lnk.href    = url;
				head.insertBefore(lnk, head.lastChild);
			}else if(tag == "script"){

				lnk.src     = url;

					lnk.onload = onload;
				}
				head.insertBefore(lnk, head.lastChild);
			}
		}
	}

function getCookieCadun() {
	var sexo = 'SEXO';

	if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
		c_start = document.cookie.indexOf(sexo + "=");
		if (c_start != -1) {
			c_start = c_start + sexo.length + 1;
			c_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";",c_start);
			if (c_end == -1) {
				c_end = document.cookie.length;
			}
			return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start,c_end));
		}
	}
	
	return 'sem-info';
}
